I'd rather have all that gunk drawn out though then left to its own devices to become a massive zit that is 10x worse and takes longer to clear up.<br /><br />I found that applying it with a foundation brush (I bought an E.L.F $1.00 one at Target just for this mask) is so much easier than applying it with your fingers and makes applying an even layer (with the least amount of product needed) a breeze. My blackheads were as clear as they've been in ages! My skin looked radiant and glowy!<br /><br />After using clay masks I always brace myself for some breakouts, however, 3 days later I have yet to have any new breakouts and the two zits I had before using this mask are completely gone.<br /><br />I'm surprisingly impressed with this product so I ordered a full size straight away.
